!

! Beam characteristics for the CNGS beam at extraction

! r.m.s. momentum spread is given

!

!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!



Beam, particle = proton, pc = 400.0,exn=12.0e-6*4.0, eyn=7.0E-6*4.0,

sige=0.4e-3, NPART=2E10, BUNCHED;



Z:=1;

A:=1;

TBUNCH:=0.5e-9;

DPP:=BEAM->SIGE*(BEAM->ENERGY/BEAM->PC)^2;



value, dpp;

dpp =    0.0004000022009 ;
return;

!! NORTH extraction

!! The ZS are horizontal kickers made of tungsten wires.

!! it is assumed that the aperture is symmetric (CERN SL-98-055 BT)

!! The TPST (protection element upstream) is on the same line of the MSTs (CERN SL-98-055 BT)

!! MSEs have an offset with respect to the girder position

!! The aperture settings have been taken from operational files (see following):

!! http://cern-accelerators-optics.web.cern.ch/cern-accelerators-optics/SPS/position_septa.xls  B.Balhan

!! WEST EXTRACTION(LSS6)

!! MSE, for the circulating beam there is virtually no vertical aperture limitation.

!! It is assumed that the aperture is symmetric

!! MSEs have an offset with respect to the girder position (CERN SL-98-055 BT).

!! The TPSG (protection element upstream) is on the same line of the MSTs (B. Balhan 23/09/03)

!! The aperture settings have been taken from operational files (see following):

!! http://cern-accelerators-optics.web.cern.ch/cern-accelerators-optics/SPS/position_septa.xls  B.Balhan

LSD       : SEXTUPOLE   , L := .42;       ! Sextupole lens, chromaticity correction, defocussing

LSE       : SEXTUPOLE   , L := .74;       ! Sextupole lens, extraction

LSEN      : SEXTUPOLE   , L := .72;       ! Sextupole lens, extraction, new magnet

LSF       : SEXTUPOLE   , L := .423;      ! Sextupole lens, chromaticity correction, focussing

//---------------------- VKICKER        ---------------------------------------------

MDV       : VKICKER     , L := .25;       ! Correcting dipole, vertical deflection

MDVA      : VKICKER     , L := .424;      ! Correcting dipole, vertical deflection, enlarged

MDVB      : VKICKER     , L := .41;       ! Correcting dipole, vertical deflection, enlarged, for BIPV upstream

MDVW      : VKICKER     , L := .526;      ! Correcting dipole, vertical deflection  (former IMHV ISR,TI)

MKDVA     : VKICKER     , L := 2.892;     ! Kicker magnet, vertical deflection for dumping, A-type

MKDVB     : VKICKER     , L := 2.892;     ! Kicker magnet, vertical deflection for dumping, B-type

MKQV      : VKICKER     , L := 1.416;     ! Kicker magnet, Q-measurement, vertical

MPLV      : VKICKER     , L := .555;      ! Bumper magnet, pulsed, long, vertical deflection

MPSV      : VKICKER     , L := .275;      ! Bumper magnet, pulsed, short, vertical deflection

ZKV       : VKICKER     , L := 1.002;     ! Electrostatic kicker, vertical (RF group)

//---------------------- VMONITOR       ---------------------------------------------

BDV       : VMONITOR    , L := 1.46;      ! Beam damper vertical (RF equipment)

BPSV      : VMONITOR    , L := 3.38;      ! Beam position, Schottky, vertical (RF group)

BPV       : VMONITOR    , L := .275;      ! Beam position, vertical

BPVC      : VMONITOR    , L := .275;      ! Beam position, vertical, short 562

BPVT      : VMONITOR    , L := .4;        ! Beam position, vertical, special short

BPW       : VMONITOR    , L := .86;       ! Pick-up station, wide band (RF group)

BPWA      : VMONITOR    , L := .86;       ! Pick-up station, wide band (RF group)

BPWB      : VMONITOR    , L := .86;       ! Pick-up station, wide band (RF group)





return;

/**************************************************************************************

 * SECTOR 2

 **************************************************************************************/



!! NORTH extraction

!! The ZS are horizontal kickers made of tungsten wires.

!! it is assumed that the aperture is symmetric (CERN SL-98-055 BT)

!! The TPST (protection element upstream) is on the same line of the MSTs (CERN SL-98-055 BT)

!! MSEs have an offset with respect to the girder position

!! The aperture settings have been taken from operational files (see following):

!! http://cern-accelerators-optics.web.cern.ch/cern-accelerators-optics/SPS/position_septa.xls  B.Balhan





Select, flag=seqedit, pattern="^ZS.21633$";

ap.UP.ZS21633:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={67.9/1000,0.046/2};

ap.DO.ZS21633:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={63.8/1000,0.046/2};



!!ap.UP.ZS21633:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={67.7/1000,0.046/2};

!!ap.DO.ZS21633:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={63.34/1000,0.046/2};





Install, element=ap.do.ZS21633, at:=ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Install, element=ap.up.ZS21633, at:=-ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Select, flag=seqedit, clear = true;



Select, flag=seqedit, pattern="^ZS.21638$";

ap.UP.ZS21638:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={62.73/1000,0.046/2};

ap.DO.ZS21638:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={58.62/1000,0.046/2};

Install, element=ap.do.ZS21638, at:=ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Install, element=ap.up.ZS21638, at:=-ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Select, flag=seqedit, clear = true;



Select, flag=seqedit, pattern="^ZS.21655$";

ap.UP.ZS21655:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={57.55/1000,0.046/2};

ap.DO.ZS21655:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={53.45/1000,0.046/2};

Install, element=ap.do.ZS21655, at:=ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Install, element=ap.up.ZS21655, at:=-ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Select, flag=seqedit, clear = true;



Select, flag=seqedit, pattern="^ZS.21671$";

ap.UP.ZS21671:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={52.38/1000,0.046/2};

ap.DO.ZS21671:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={48.27/1000,0.046/2};

Install, element=ap.do.ZS21671, at:=ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Install, element=ap.up.ZS21671, at:=-ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Select, flag=seqedit, clear = true;



Select, flag=seqedit, pattern="^ZS.21676$";

ap.UP.ZS21676:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={47.20/1000,0.046/2};

ap.DO.ZS21676:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={43.10/1000,0.046/2};

Install, element=ap.do.ZS21676, at:=ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Install, element=ap.up.ZS21676, at:=-ZS->l/2, from=selected;

Select, flag=seqedit, clear = true;





Select, flag=seqedit, pattern="^TPST.21759$";

ap.UP.TPST21759:AP,APERTYPE=RECTANGLE,APERTURE={39.40/1000,0.078};
